{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2021-04-10 00:41:45","updatedTime":"2021-04-10 00:41:45","title":"How the Google VPN service works to give Google One users added security online","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/google-one-vpn","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606f315f30004b0019b26acc?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Phone VPN in coffee shop\" height=\"1414\" width=\"1885\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Google&#39;s VPN service offers online protection when you&#39;re using an unsecured public network.\n<p class=\"copyright\">mihailomilovanovic/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>VPN by Google One provides extra security and anonymity whenever you&#39;re online via a private encryption connection. </li>\n<li>Google&#39;s VPN service hides your IP address so your activity can&#39;t be tracked online and protects your device against hackers when you&#39;re on an unsecured public network. </li>\n<li>The Google VPN costs $9.99 per month and is only available in the U.S.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tech-reference\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Visit Insider&#39;s Tech Reference library for more stories</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Protecting yourself and your private data when you&#39;re online has never been more critical. One of the best ways to do this is via a virtual private network or VPN. </p><bi-shortcode id=\"related-article-module\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-type=\"5f0f55c6191824089a3d9df4\" data-title=\"What is a VPN? How a Virtual Private Network can help protect your privacy online\" data-url=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/what-is-vpn\" data-thumbnail=\"https://i.insider.com/undefined\">Related Article Module: What is a VPN? How a Virtual Private Network can help protect your privacy online</bi-shortcode><p>VPNs create private internet connections across public networks, not only keeping your IP address confidential but ensuring that others can&#39;t gain access to your devices and allowing you to navigate the internet without being tracked. </p><p>Companies like NordVPN and ExpressVPN have offered a subscription-based VPN service for many years, but Google is getting in on the security game with its new VPN by Google One service. </p><h2>What is VPN by Google One </h2><p>Available exclusively to people in the United States for $9.99 per month, those who purchase the monthly subscription get access to several services and online security benefits - all tied directly to your Google account. </p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606f333b4d3e410018b70075?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Google One VPN 1\" height=\"1291\" width=\"2363\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Google One&#39;s VPN service offers online security for Android users.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Abbey White/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>That includes increased security, allowing you to download and stream via a private encrypted internet connection and protect against hackers on public networks such as a coffee shop or library&#39;s WiFi connection. Users also get a shielded IP address so that no one can track them by their location. </p><h2>How the Google VPN works </h2><p>Unlike some other VPN programs, using Google&#39;s VPN service doesn&#39;t require any special configuration.</p><p>Instead, it&#39;s accessed via the Google One app and can be turned on and off within the Benefits menu. Simply toggle the VPN option to the on position when you want to use it and tap again when you want to turn it off. </p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606f352130004b0019b26ae5?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Google One VPN 2\" height=\"1145\" width=\"720\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Just toggle on the VPN in the Google One app to instantly get online protection.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Abbey White/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>According to Google, the VPN won&#39;t slow down your internet connection, nor will it track or sell your browsing history or use your connection to personally identify you. </p><h2>What you need to use the Google One VPN</h2><p>At present, the Google VPN service is only available on Android devices. However, on the VPN&#39;s site, Google does note plans to expand the service to iOS, ChromeOS, Windows, and Mac in the near future. </p><p>Using Google&#39;s VPN service requires you to have a paid <a href=\"https://one.google.com/about/plans\">Google One storage plan</a> of 2 TB, with the service automatically included at no additional cost. It is easily accessible through the Google One app.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606f358a30004b0019b26aed?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Google One VPN 3\" height=\"920\" width=\"720\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>You can find the VPN under the Google One Benefits tab.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Abbey White/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>As an added feature, your Google One VPN connection can be set up simultaneously across six separate devices per plan, so long as the Google One app is installed on each of them. </p><bi-shortcode id=\"related-article-module-end-of-article\" only 220 cd/㎡, non-touchscreen panel</p><p>Asus touts the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B071S84ZW7/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_060319_best-portable-monitors-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B071S84ZW7&#38;linkId=b0ceca946bbc61aff8316c1d633736ab\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Asus ZenScreen MB16AC</a> as a super slim and light portable monitor, which it is. It's almost half the thinness and weight of the new MacBook Pro 13-inch at 8 millimeters and 0.78 kilograms, making it a glorious companion when you're traveling or working on-the-go. But, it's also so much more than that.</p><p>This portable monitor claims to be the world's first portable monitor with a hybrid-signal solution, meaning that not only does it have native USB-C support, but it also offers USB-A connectivity support via the DisplayLink driver. So, whether you're entirely dependent on USB-C or you find yourself needing to use a USB-A connection every now and then, this offers that versatility you need.</p><p>Its vibrant 15.6-inch IPS screen with a 1080p (1,920 x 1,080-pixel) resolution also allows automatic screen orientation with the DisplayWidget software. That means you can switch from landscape mode for productivity to portrait mode for presentations and reading.&#160;</p><p>Besides the automatic screen orientation, it also has its own foldable smart case to protect the screen from scratches and dust, a smart pen hole so you won't lose another stylus pen, and the Asus blue light filter so it's easy on the eyes. And, it comes with its own ZenScreen pen.</p>\n\tThe best budget portable monitor\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f3bf67d650894001d0721d0?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Auzai monitor\" monitor title.&#160;</p><p>Among its features are compatibility with PlayStation and Xbox game consoles &#8212; which should apply to the previous and current generation models &#8212; its own built-in speakers, and a settings menu so you can adjust brightness, contrast and&#160; audio based on your personal preferences. It may only have a 60Hz refresh rate, but that's certainly enough for casual gaming.</p><p>This 15.6-inch 1080p IPS portable monitor is also incredibly sleek, beating the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B071S84ZW7/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_060319_best-portable-monitors-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B071S84ZW7&#38;linkId=b0ceca946bbc61aff8316c1d633736ab\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Asus ZenScreen MB16AC</a> at 3.56 millimeters thin and 0.62 kilograms. The sound quality isn't the best, understandably due to its thinness, but the picture quality is excellent with deep contrast, vibrant colors, and decent brightness at 250 cd/m&#178;.</p><p>It's certainly a great portable viewing solution for gaming and entertainment. And, thanks to the case and screen protector that come with it, you know it'll stay safe in your bag while you're on-the-go.</p>\n\tThe best portable monitor for 4K HDR\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f3bf7aea3eafa001de06bb6?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Eviciv monitor\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Amazon</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3><strong>The </strong><a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B0828CXGN7/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_060319_best-portable-monitors-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B0828CXGN7&#38;linkId=701e7239ea1edc00da24be44b52bd97e\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\"><strong>Eviciv 4K Portable Monitor</strong></a><strong> comes at a solid price for a 4K portable monitor and has many features to offer.</strong></h3><aside class=\"breakout-box headline-regular\"><ul><li><strong>Screen size:</strong> 15.6-inches</li><li><strong>Resolution:</strong> 4K, 3840 x 1260p</li><li><strong>Connectivity:</strong> 2 USB-C, mini HDMI</li><li><strong>Refresh rate:</strong> 60Hz</li><li>Check out our guide to the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-mouse\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">best computer mouse</a></li></ul></aside><p><strong>Pros:</strong> Really affordable for everything it offers, excellent 4K picture quality, 178-degree viewing angle, great feature set, nice port selection</p><p><strong>Cons:</strong> There are cheaper alternatives if you don't need 4K resolution</p><p>While 4K resolution (3,840 x 2,160 pixels) is all the rage in computer monitors these days, portable 4K monitors are rare. There's a good reason why: These monitors are small enough that having 1080p resolution is actually much better, especially for productivity.&#160;</p><p>However, if 4K is necessary for your workflow,the 15.6-inch <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B0828CXGN7/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_060319_best-portable-monitors-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B0828CXGN7&#38;linkId=701e7239ea1edc00da24be44b52bd97e\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Eviciv 4K Portable Monitor</a> is the most cost-effective option.</p><p>It offers 300cd/m&#178; brightness, 16.7 million display colors, and 100% sRGB colour gamut, giving photographers and video editors vibrant images with accurate colors.</p><p>The monitor also has a 178-degree viewing angle, HDR support, AMD FreeSync for gamers, portrait and landscape modes for presentations, and built-in speakers for entertainment. It also includes a nice selection of connections, including one HDMI and 2 <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/what-is-usb-c\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">USB-C</a> ports that offer both power and signal support.&#160;</p><p>And, if those features aren't enough, it also comes with a nifty magnetic stand cover. Not bad for a portable monitor that's less than $350? We'd say it's a bargain.</p>\n\tThe best portable monitor for gaming\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f3bfafd650894001d0721f1?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Asus Rog Monitor\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">B&#38;H</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>For esports and fast-paced gaming, you cannot go wrong with the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B0845Y1FRN/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_060319_best-portable-monitors-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B0845Y1FRN&#38;linkId=0a4bb1ab463e4d515319986e892734de\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Asus ROG Strix XG17AHPE</a>, as long as you can put up with its massive size.</h3><aside class=\"breakout-box headline-regular\"><ul><li><strong>Screen size:</strong> 17.3-inches</li><li><strong>Resolution:</strong> 4K, 3840 x 1260p</li><li><strong>Connectivity:</strong> 2 USB-C, mini HDMI</li><li><strong>Refresh rate:</strong> 240Hz</li><li>Check out our guide to the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-gaming-headset\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">best gaming headset</a></li></ul></aside><p><strong>Pros:</strong> Incredibly fast refresh rate, not too expensive, up to three hours of battery life, nice port selection</p><p><strong>Cons:</strong> Big, heavier than most portable monitors</p><p>The <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B0845Y1FRN/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_060319_best-portable-monitors-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B0845Y1FRN&#38;linkId=0a4bb1ab463e4d515319986e892734de\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Asus ROG Strix XG17AHPE</a> is the most advanced portable monitor you'll find, especially if you're all about fast-paced gaming and esports.&#160;</p><p>With its 240Hz refresh rate and 3-millisecond response time, it delivers the smoothest picture quality you'll find in a portable display. That's on top of its adaptive-sync technology, which enables tear-free gaming for a more immersive experience, and a 17.3-inch IPS panel for more space.</p><p>Even better, this screen offers up to three hours of battery life when gaming at 240Hz. It also offers a wide 178-degree viewing angle that's ideal for esports players gaming in front of an audience.&#160;</p><p>It also includes other perks like 100% sRGB color gamut for a rich and vibrant display quality, quick charging capabilities, built-in stereo speakers, and a decent selection of ports that include <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/what-is-usb-c\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">USB-C</a>, micro HDMI and a 3.5mm audio jack. And of course, it comes with Asus' ROG Smart Cover for protection.</p><p>It's somehow even cheaper than the MSI Optix MAG161V, though not by much. Just know that this is a 17-inch display weighing 1.06 kilograms, which makes it too bulky for light travel.</p>\n\tThe best touchscreen portable monitor\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/5f3bfc38650894001d0721fe?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Asus MOnitor 2\" height=\"900\" width=\"1200\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">B&#38;H</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<h3>Windows and Android users will love the immersive touchscreen experience on the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B07WC2NL2G/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_060319_best-portable-monitors-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B07WC2NL2G&#38;linkId=239857a086f49d6cb0529ad6a25ab06c\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Asus Zenscreen MB16AMT</a>.</h3><aside class=\"breakout-box headline-regular\"><ul><li><strong>Screen size:</strong> 15.6-inches</li><li><strong>Resolution:</strong> 1080p</li><li><strong>Connectivity:</strong> USB-C, mini HDMI</li><li><strong>Refresh rate:</strong> 60Hz</li><li>Check out our guide to the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-charging-cables\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">best charging cables</a></li></ul></aside><p><strong>Pros: </strong>Touchscreen capability is impeccable, decent battery life, nice feature set, fairly lightweight, great picture quality</p><p><strong>Cons: </strong>Single port, a bit pricey, touchscreen support for macOS limited</p><p>Touchscreen support is pretty much standard on today's laptops, even those that aren't meant to be laptop-tablet hybrids. So it was only a matter of time before touchscreens became available on portable monitors as well.&#160;</p><p>The best one we've seen so far is the <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B07WC2NL2G/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&#38;tag=biipgf_060319_best-portable-monitors-20&#38;camp=1789&#38;creative=9325&#38;linkCode=as2&#38;creativeASIN=B07WC2NL2G&#38;linkId=239857a086f49d6cb0529ad6a25ab06c\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored\">Asus Zenscreen MB16AMT</a>, which comes with gesture-based, multi-touch controls that are simply fantastic.</p><p>Smooth, accurate, and responsive, especially on Windows and Android, this 15.6-inch IPS touchscreen portable monitor is the one to get, especially if you're using it for design.</p><p>The monitor also has a 7,800mAh battery that can last for up to four hours, and it's fairly lightweight as well at 0.91 kilograms. We would have liked it to be a little brighter, but at 250 cd/㎡, it's luminous enough. Plus, the vibrant picture quality and superb contrast should make up for that.</p><p>Other notable features worth mentioning include its hybrid signal solution, so you can use both <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/what-is-usb-c\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">USB-C</a> and USB Type A connections, a smart cover and smart pen hole, a wide 178&#176; viewing angle, and automatic screen orientation.</p>\n\tHow to choose a portable monitor\n\t\n\t<p>Portable monitors come in a variety of sizes, prices, and connectivity types, so there's something out there for everyone. Still, there are a few key factors to consider.</p><ul><li aria-level=\"1\"><strong>Size:</strong> Just like laptops, portable monitors are typically available in 13.3-, 15.6-, and 17.3- inch sizes. Consider what it is you'll be using it for before you decide. Larger displays offer a better viewing experience so they're best for games and entertainment. However, they also tend to be heavier. If portability and traveling light are your main concerns, then a smaller screen might be a better choice.</li><li aria-level=\"1\"><strong>Resolution:</strong> The resolution of a portable monitor determines how sharp and detailed the image will look. Portable monitors are available in 4K, Full HD 1080p, and lower resolutions &#8211; though 1080p is the standard.&#160;</li><li aria-level=\"1\"><strong>Connectivity:</strong> A USB-C or Thunderbolt 3 connection is the best available. It's more powerful, has faster transfer speeds, and is becoming the standard on many laptops. However, some portable displays also include common video connections like HDMI, allowing you to easily connect them to game consoles and media players. Others still have USB ports, some of which can also be used to power the monitor directly from a connected device.</li><li aria-level=\"1\"><strong>Refresh rate and response time:</strong> If you're buying a portable monitor for gaming, you should be mindful of the display's refresh rate and response time. Refresh rates higher than 60Hz can provide a smoother experience when gaming at higher frame rates. Some portable gaming monitors come with 240Hz refresh rates, which is pretty impressive considering it outpaces frame rates in most PC games.</li></ul>\n</div><div class=\"read-original\">Read the 00:41:45","updatedTime":"2021-04-10 00:41:45","title":"The SEC says it's looking closely at the wild earnings projections attached to many SPAC offerings","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/sec-spac-earnings-wild-projections-offering-black-check-ipo-2021-4","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60704f294d3e410018b7031a?format=jpeg\" alt=\"FILE PHOTO: The U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission logo adorns an office door at the SEC headquarters in Washington, June 24, 2011. REUTERS/Jonathan Ernst\" height=\"1851\" width=\"3704\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>FILE PHOTO: The U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission logo adorns an office door\n<p class=\"copyright\">Reuters</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>The SEC is warning investors on the lofty projections that come with many SPAC offerings. </li>\n<li>The agency added it will &#34;look carefully&#34; at filings and disclosures of SPACs.</li>\n<li>The SEC said it will treat SPAC deals with the same level of scrutiny as traditional IPOs. </li>\n<li><a href=\"https://newsletter.businessinsider.com/join/4np/10-things-opening-bell\">Sign up here for our daily newsletter, 10 Things Before the Opening Bell</a></li>\n</ul><p>The US Securities and Exchange Commission issued a warning to blank-check companies presenting projections that only give an optimistic outlook of future growth. The agency added that it will &#34;look carefully&#34; at SPAC filings and disclosures as well as those of their private targets.</p><p>John Coates, the agency&#39;s acting director for the corporation finance division, said <a href=\"https://www.sec.gov/news/public-statement/spacs-ipos-liability-risk-under-securities-laws?campaign_id=4&emc=edit_dk_20210409&instance_id=29035&nl=dealbook&regi_id=85242594&segment_id=55266&te=1&user_id=b7ecb39412279947d1966b4c36d2a5e0&utm_medium=email&utm_source=govdeliveryium=email&#38;utm_source=govdelivery\">on Thursday</a> that a company would be on &#34;shaky ground&#34; if it only disclosed favorable projections and omitted &#34;equally reliable but unfavorable projections.&#34;</p><p>Special purpose acquisition companies or SPACs have been booming, enabling many pre-revenue startups to go public. SPACs are essentially shell companies seeking to merge with private companies with the intention of taking them public. SPACs are often considered a cheaper, faster alternative to a traditional IPO.</p><p>SPAC sponsors have also generally been allowed to more freely give projections of future growth than is allowed for companies going public via traditional IPO, which are not allowed to broadcast future sales or earnings.</p><p>Coates pointed to the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act safe harbor, a legal liability SPACs often refer to when making optimistic forward-looking statements. </p><p>&#34;This...is the reason that sponsors, targets, and others involved in a de-SPAC feel comfortable presenting projections and other valuation material of a kind that is not commonly found in conventional IPO prospectuses,&#34; he said, referring to the safe harbor. </p><p>This, he said, raises significant investor protection questions, and is why he is calling on the agency to treat SPAC deals with the same level of scrutiny as IPOs. </p><p>&#34;Any simple claim about reduced liability exposure for SPAC participants is overstated at best, and potentially seriously misleading at worst,&#34; Coates said. &#34;Indeed, in some ways, liability risks for those involved are higher, not lower, than in conventional IPOs, due in particular to the potential conflicts of interest in the SPAC structure.&#34;</p><p>Coates added that while projections are woven into the fabric of business combinations, they have to be fair. Forward-looking information, he said, can be &#34;untested, speculative, misleading or even fraudulent, as reflected in the limitations on the PSLRA&#39;s liability protections.&#34; He floated the possibility of having guidance about how projections and related valuations should be presented.</p><p>SPACs have attracted a number of high-profile investors including famed fund manager Bill Ackman and billionaire Chamath Palihapitiya. Celebrities have also joined the bandwagon, with icons such as baseball star Alex Rodriguez and tennis legend Serena Williams backing recent SPAC offerings. </p><p>Regulators have recently turned their eye to the soaring market. On March 11, acting SEC Chair Allison Herren Lee said that <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/spac-returns-dont-warrant-the-hype-sec-chair-says-2021-3-1030175236?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingestgestgest\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-id=\"67\" data-m=\"{\"i\":67,\"p\":62,\"n\":\"partnerLink\",\"y\":24,\"o\":5}4;partnerLink&#34;,&#34;y&#34;:24,&#34;o&#34;:5}\">SPAC returns don&#39;t warrant the &#34;hype&#34;</a> they&#39;re getting.</p><p>Last year, a total of 248 SPACs raised $83.3 billion according to <a href=\"https://www.spacanalytics.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-id=\"66\" data-m=\"{\"i\":66,\"p\":62,\"n\":\"partnerLink\",\"y\":24,\"o\":4}4;partnerLink&#34;,&#34;y&#34;:24,&#34;o&#34;:4}\">SPAC Analytics</a>. But by the fourth month of 2021 alone, data already show 306 SPACs that raised $98.3 billion, comprising 79% of all public offerings.</p><p> </p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tesla-starts-model-y-production-shanghai-china-reduces-price-2021-1\">its Shanghai, China Gigafactory</a>.</p><figure>\n\t<img door panel.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Tesla</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>Customers told CNBC that <a had double-charged for new cars</a> in mid-March, leaving them with bills of up to $142,000.</p><p>A Tesla customer, Terry Oelschlaeger, <a $54,000 on March 25, and that a Tesla service center employee told him the error had affected &#34;many&#34; buyers.</p><p>The company has since <a online store.</p><p>Tesla posted <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tesla-q1-deliveries-car-sales-chip-shortage-headwinds-2021-4?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingestgest\" in <a interview with The Washington Post</a> said that President Joe Biden believes it&#39;s in the world&#39;s best interest for the US to act as a global leader. </p><p>&#34;What he sees time and again is that ... when we&#39;re not leading,&#34; then another country, often China, &#34;tries to assert itself in our place&#34; and this can be harmful to US interests, Blinken said. &#34;Or no one shows up&#34; and it leads to &#34;chaos and law of the jungle,&#34; the secretary of state added. </p><p>Former President Donald Trump had a starkly different perspective on foreign affairs, as evidenced by his &#34;America First&#34; philosophy. Trump often took a unilateral approach to foreign policy, pulling the US out of major agreements and railing against international institutions the US played a key role in establishing, like the United Nations and NATO. Experts and diplomats warned that Trump&#39;s handling of foreign policy <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/trump-chaotic-coronavirus-response-has-created-void-china-is-filling-2020-4\">created a void in global leadership that China was rapidly filling.</a></p><p>Blinken&#39;s summary of Biden&#39;s foreign policy to The Post presented a picture of a president with a decidedly traditional, but also pragmatic worldview. Biden believes the US should be at the helm in terms of global leadership, which includes challenging China and Russia, but also views cooperation and compromise as crucial aspects of effective foreign policy.</p><p>&#34;The president is very clear-eyed about two things,&#34; Blinken told the Post: He must &#34;hold Russia to account for any reckless or adversarial actions it takes&#34; while simultaneously remaining open to &#34;areas in which it may be in our mutual interest to work with Russia.&#34; Biden recently referred to Russian President Vladimir Putin, whose critics often wind up dead or seriously harmed, as a &#34;killer.&#34; This prompted outrage from the Kremlin. </p><p>Blinken, who got into a <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/biden-proud-of-blinken-after-confrontation-with-chinas-top-diplomat-2021-3\">public spat with China&#39;s top diplomat in Alaska</a> last month after bringing up the Chinese government&#39;s human rights abuses, also said it&#39;s not the goal of the US to &#34;contain China, hold China back, keep it down.&#34;</p><p>This, however, deviates from <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/biden-says-wont-let-china-become-most-wealthy-powerful-country-2021-3\">Biden&#39;s recent messaging on China</a>. The president in a recent speech, for example, said that he wouldn&#39;t let China become the wealthiest, most powerful country in the world. </p><p>&#34;They have an overall goal to become the leading country in the world, the wealthiest country in the world, and the most powerful country in the world. That&#39;s not gonna happen on my watch,&#34; Biden said of China. </p><p>The president has made challenging China a top foreign policy goal, <a href=\"https://www.cnn.com/2021/03/22/politics/us-eu-china-uyghur-sanctions/index.html\">condemning the Chinese government&#39;s human rights violations</a> while pushing for <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/biden-suggests-gop-aiding-china-by-opposing-infrastructure-plan-2021-4\">investments in infrastructure</a> and underscoring the importance of making the US more competitive in technology and science. </p><p>&#34;Do you think China is waiting around to invest in its digital infrastructure or research and development? I promise you, they are not waiting,&#34; Biden said in a speech earlier this week touting his $2 trillion infrastructure proposal. &#34;But they are counting on American democracy to be too slow, too limited, and too divided to keep up the pace.&#34;</p><p>The Biden administration this week also took steps to derail China&#39;s effort to build the world&#39;s fastest supercomputer, necessary for the development of virtually-unstoppable hypersonic missiles and other advanced weapons. </p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a 00:41:45","updatedTime":"2021-04-10 00:41:45","title":"Billionaire investor Peter Thiel called out Apple and Google, warned about TikTok and bitcoin, and criticized China at a recent event. Here are the 17 best quotes.","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/peter-thiel-criticizes-apple-google-warns-tiktok-bitcoin-china-threat-2021-4","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/540ff874eab8ea281c65a625?format=jpeg\" alt=\"peter thiel\" height=\"2808\" width=\"5616\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Peter Thiel.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Chip Somodevilla / Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul><li><strong>Peter Thiel called out Apple and Google for their links to China this week.</strong></li><li><strong>The billionaire tech investor issued warnings about bitcoin, TikTok, and AI.</strong></li><li><strong>Thiel wants to restrict US investors&#39; access to Chinese markets and vice versa.</strong></li><li><strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</strong></li></ul><p>Billionaire investor <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/peter-thiel-facebook-trump-biography-2018-2\">Peter Thiel</a> warned bitcoin <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/currencies/news/peter-thiel-bitcoin-chinese-financial-weapon-against-us-threatens-dollar-2021-4-1030284380\">could serve</a> as a &#34;Chinese financial weapon,&#34; criticized Apple and Google for their <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/tech-companies-censoring-content-for-china-apple-microsoft-2019-10\">connections to China</a>, and suggested TikTok should be <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/donald-trump-tiktok-ban-us-china-explained-in-30-seconds-2020-8\">banned</a> in the US at a <a href=\"https://nixonseminar.com/2021/04/the-nixon-seminar-april-6-2021-transcript\">virtual event held by the Richard Nixon Foundation</a> this week.</p><p>Thiel, the vocal libertarian who co-founded PayPal and Palantir and sits on the board of Facebook Facebook board member, also expressed concerns about technology theft and artificial intelligence, and called for greater restrictions on Chinese investment in the US and vice versa.</p><p>The event was called &#34;The Nixon Seminar on Conservative Realism and National Security,&#34; and the topic of discussion was &#34;Big Tech and China: What do we need from Silicon Valley?&#34;</p><h2>Here are Thiel&#39;s 17 best quotes from the seminar, lightly edited and condensed for clarity:</h2><p><strong>1.</strong> &#34;Shockingly little innovation happens in China. But they have been very good at copying things, stealing things.&#34;</p><p><strong>2.</strong> &#34;I criticized Google a few years ago for working with Chinese universities and Chinese researchers. And since everything in China is a civilian-military fusion, Google was effectively working with the Chinese military. One of the things that I was sort of told by some of the insiders at Google was they figured they might as well give the technology out the front door, because if they didn&#39;t give it, it would get stolen anyway.&#34;</p><p><strong>3.</strong> &#34;I had a set of conversations with some of the DeepMind AI people at Google. I asked them, &#39;Is your AI being used to run the concentration camps in Xinjiang?&#39; and they said, &#39;Well, we don&#39;t know and don&#39;t ask any questions.&#39; You have this almost magical thinking that by pretending everything is fine, that&#39;s how you engage and have a conversation, and you make the world better.&#34; - <em>A DeepMind spokesperson told Insider: &#34;This claim is entirely false. We have never worked with the Chinese military and have been clear since DeepMind was founded that our research and technology is intended for use in ways that are beneficial to society.&#34;</em></p><p><strong>4.</strong> &#34;If you look at the big five tech companies, Google, Facebook, Amazon, and Microsoft all have very, very little presence in China. So they aren&#39;t a naturally pro-China constituency. Apple is probably the one that&#39;s structurally a real problem, because the whole iPhone supply chain gets made from China.&#34;</p><p><strong>5.</strong> &#34;We need to call companies like Google out for working on AI with communist China. I also think we should be putting a lot of pressure on Apple.&#34;</p><p><strong>6.</strong> &#34;At Facebook, during the Hong Kong protests a year ago, the employees from Hong Kong were all in favor of the protests and free speech. But there were more employees at Facebook who were born in China than who were born in Hong Kong. And the Chinese nationals actually said that it was just Western arrogance, and they shouldn&#39;t be taking Hong Kong&#39;s side and things like that. The internal debate felt like people were actually more anti-Hong Kong than pro-Hong Kong.&#34;</p><p><em><strong>Read more:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/crypto-arbitrage-trading-strategy-alameda-research-sam-bankman-fried-billionaire-2021-4\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">A 29-year-old self-made billionaire breaks down how he achieved daily returns of 10% on million-dollar crypto trades, and shares how to find the best opportunities</a></em></p><p><strong>7.</strong> &#34;TikTok is problematic because it has this incredible exfiltration of data about people. You are creating this incredibly privacy-invading map of a large part of the population of the Western world. It is a fairly powerful application of AI in a certain sense, as they find ways to make it especially addictive and figure out what videos to show you to keep you watching more and more. It doesn&#39;t seem that if you shut it down, it would be an economic catastrophe.&#34;</p><p><strong>8.</strong> &#34;In a totalitarian society, you have no qualms about getting data on everybody, in every way possible. That makes AI a very tricky technology, because there are a lot of ways we don&#39;t actually want to apply it in the US or West.&#34; - <em>highlighting the Chinese government&#39;s use of AI for widescale facial recognition.</em></p><p><strong>9.</strong> &#34;People often say crypto or bitcoin is a vaguely libertarian technology. If crypto is kind of libertarian, AI is kind of communist.&#34;</p><p><strong>10.</strong> &#34;Even though I&#39;m sort of a pro-crypto, pro-bitcoin maximalist person, I do wonder whether bitcoin should be partly thought of as a Chinese financial weapon against the US. It threatens fiat money, especially the US dollar, and China wants to do things to weaken the dollar. If China&#39;s long bitcoin, perhaps the US should be asking some tougher questions about exactly how that works.&#34;</p><p><strong>11.</strong> &#34;An internal stable coin in China - that&#39;s not a real cryptocurrency. That&#39;s just some sort of totalitarian measuring device.&#34;</p><p><strong>12.</strong> &#34;Make it harder for Chinese investors to invest in the US, and perhaps we should also make it a little bit harder for American investors to invest in China. We have US investors that invest in China and become a big constituency for open capital flows. I think a decent part of the Wall Street crowd is pretty bad in this regard. I would dial it back on both sides - making it harder for US investors to invest in China is an almost equally important part of this.&#34;<br><br><strong>13.</strong> &#34;China doesn&#39;t like the US having the reserve currency, because it gives us a lot of leverage over Iranian oil supply chains and all sorts of things like that. You can think of the Euro in part as a Chinese weapon against the dollar. China would have liked to see two reserve currencies.&#34;</p><p><strong>14.</strong> &#34;One of the very strange dynamics in Silicon Valley is people don&#39;t do very much with semiconductors anymore. One of the weird problems with 20 years of intellectual property theft, and where IP doesn&#39;t really have as much value as it used to, is that you learn not to invest in things like that.&#34;</p><p><em><strong>Read more:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/goldman-sachs-stock-picks-for-higher-eps-earnings-growth-consensus-2021-4\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Goldman Sachs handpicks 40 stocks that will enjoy bigger earnings growth than Wall Street expects in 2021</a></em></p><p><strong>15.</strong> &#34;People are too anchored to doing things that worked in the past or copying some model. Building a new search engine was the right thing for Google to do in 1999. It&#39;s probably not the right thing to do today. It&#39;s very hard to compete against Google by doing the exact same thing they are doing.&#34;</p><p><strong>16.</strong> &#34;You can think of big tech as something that&#39;s very natural. It&#39;s maybe unnaturally big. It&#39;s unhealthy. It&#39;s too strong. But there&#39;s something in the nature of tech to be big. Big science is actually an oxymoron. business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>John Boehner, the former Republican House Speaker, wrote in his forthcoming memoir that he regrets supporting former President Bill Clinton&#39;s impeachment, which he said was a purely political effort. </p><p>Clinton&#39;s 1998 impeachment for lying about his affair with White House intern Monica Lewinsky was orchestrated by Texas Rep. Tom DeLay, the second highest-ranking Republican in the House at the time, Boehner wrote.</p><p data-el=\"text\">&#34;I know what we all said at the time: Bill Clinton was impeached for lying under oath,&#34; Boehner wrote, according to an excerpt of &#34;On the House: A Washington Memoir,&#34; obtained by <a href=\"https://www.washingtonpost.com/politics/john-boehner-book/2021/04/08/3316e808-9877-11eb-b28d-bfa7bb5cb2a5_story.html\">The Washington Post</a> and <a href=\"https://www.nytimes.com/2021/04/08/us/politics/boehner-clinton-impeachment.html\">The New York Times</a>. &#34;In my view, Republicans impeached him for one reason and one reason only - because it was strenuously recommended to us by one Tom DeLay.&#34;</p><p data-el=\"text\">He added: &#34;Tom believed that impeaching Clinton would win us all these House seats, would be a big win politically, and he convinced enough of the membership and the GOP base that this was true.&#34; </p><p data-el=\"text\">Clinton&#39;s impeachment didn&#39;t end up helping the GOP in the midterms - the party lost five House seats in 1998. </p><p data-el=\"text\">Boehner concedes that he supported the impeachment effort - the House ultimately impeached Clinton on two charges before the Senate acquitted him - but now regrets it. He added that Clinton likely committed perjury, but that &#34;lying about an affair to save yourself from embarrassment isn&#39;t the same as lying about an issue of national security.&#34;  </p><p data-el=\"text\">&#34;I was on board at the time,&#34; Boehner wrote. &#34;I won&#39;t pretend otherwise. have been at any point in the pandemic. He said the bank needs to &#34;eliminate the stigma associated with asking for time to focus, concentrate, and in some cases, log off and recharge.&#34;</p><p>McKay told employees in the memo they should speak to their managers to book the extra day off and encouraged them to take the time to go on vacation. He said the few vacations he&#39;d taken in the pandemic had allowed him to read, play his guitar, and spend more time outside.</p><p>Canada&#39;s second-biggest bank also offered its global workforce of around 86,000 workers a free one-year subscription to Headspace, which usually <a href=\"https://www.headspace.com/subscriptions?gclid=CjwKCAjw9r-DBhBxEiwA9qYUpXlpH4gbUYZI45K3Xexhj15ZyPYoytNGhTIsK6xcmmGdpHQjwKwB_xoCLbQQAvD_BwE\">costs $69.99</a>.</p><p>&#34;Beyond this extra day off, we recognize the ongoing pressures of the pandemic, especially for those in regions that have reverted back into lockdown,&#34; McKay said. Canada is currently in a <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/canada-3rd-covid-19-wave-young-people-new-variants-2021-4\">third wave of coronavirus infections</a> which has mainly hit the province of Ontario, where RBC headquarters are. The province has introduced new restrictions to stop the spread.</p><p>&#34;I encourage all of you to prioritize your personal time and continue to be mindful about work-life boundaries wherever possible,&#34; McKay told staff in the memo.</p><p>Toronto-Dominion Bank, Canada&#39;s largest bank, has also told staff they would get an extra day off work. CEO Bharat Masrani said in a memo to staff, seen by Bloomberg, that they should take the day off when they need it the most. </p><p>&#34;After a year of sacrifice and disruption, we must all endure these challenging circumstances for a bit longer,&#34; Masrani said in the memo. &#34;I know that this has not been easy, and everyone is tired.&#34;</p><p>The bank&#39;s decisions to give staff an additional day off come after Goldman Sachs was criticized for making <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/goldman-sachs-junior-bankers-inhumane-working-conditions-survey-2021-3\">junior bankers work 100-hour weeks</a> in &#34;inhumane&#34; conditions, leading to poor mental health.</p><p>Citigroup also launched a <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/citigroup-ceo-jane-fraser-bans-friday-video-calls-zoom-vacation-2021-3\">&#34;Citi Reset Day&#34;</a> on March 28 - a company-wide holiday to relieve stress on staff. CEO Jane Fraser also banned video calls on a Friday.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a earnings and a booming sales forecast. Analysts from UBS also predict the stock will surge another 25% from current levels.</p><p>Levi was up 4.62% to $26.17 as of 11:05 a.m. ET, having risen to a session peak of $27.17 earlier in the day, its highest since it listed in March 2019. </p><p>The San Francisco-based company <a href=\"https://investors.levistrauss.com/news/financial-news/news-details/2021/Levi-Strauss--Co.-Reports-First-Quarter-2021-Financial-Results/default.aspx\">on Thursday</a> reported an overall 13% net revenue decline for the first quarter of 2021 ending February 28, largely to the ongoing closures of retail locations in select locations and decreased foot traffic overall as more people stayed at home to curb the spread of the virus. More than 40% of the full store footprint in Europe is closed, with others operating on reduced hours, the company said.</p><p>The company, however, raised its sales and profit outlook for the second quarter of 2021 on optimist of an economic recovery. The comany said net revenue could increase 24%-25% in the first half of fiscal 2021 compared with the same period a year ago - a jump from its initial guidance of 18%-20%.</p><p>&#34;We are banking the outperformance and our outlook going forward has improved based on the strong demand signals we are seeing in the marketplace,&#34; Harmit Singh, company CFO, <a href=\"https://investors.levistrauss.com/news/financial-news/news-details/2021/Levi-Strauss--Co.-Reports-First-Quarter-2021-Financial-Results/default.aspx\">said in a statement</a>. &#34;This gives me confidence we&#39;ll achieve our adjusted EBIT margin objective of 12 percent-plus once revenues have returned to pre-pandemic levels.&#34;</p><p>The company also raised its quarterly dividend to $0.06 per share from $0.04, payable on May 25 to holders of record on May 7.</p><p>Levis reported adjusted earnings per share of $0.34 compared to the $0.25 <a href=\"https://www.cnbc.com/2021/04/08/levis-levi-reports-q1-2021-earnings.html\">analysts</a> expected, and a $1.31 billion revenue compared to the $1.25 billion forecast.</p><p>On Friday, UBS analyst Jay Sole raised his price target for the company by 17% to $34 from $29. He maintains his buy rating for the denim brand. </p><p>&#34;The market doesn&#39;t fully appreciate the positive impact on Levi&#39;s future earnings from the combined power of reopening, an emerging denim cycle, brand investments, mix shifts, and cost savings,&#34; Sole said.</p><p>The analyst said he expects Levi&#39;s earnings per share to reach $1.60 in 2023 - 43% above Levi&#39;s pre-pandemic level and 10% ahead of consensus. He said this type of growth plus regular earnings beats will cause the stock&#39;s price-to-earnings ratio to rise to 21x from 19.7x. </p><p>Levi in 2019 went public for the second time. The 168-year-old company previously went public in 1971 but its namesake founders, 14 years after, took it private again.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a data-pid=\"5e625a28fee23d701e01546c\" data-purchase-option=\"\">Home Starter Pack (small)</bi-shortcode><p>I won&#39;t go into much detail here, but you can probably paint the picture in your mind: on a cold, rainy February evening back in 2017, my father-in-law and I were frantically taking turns manning a pair of wet/dry vacuums as we fought to keep a flood contained to a basement room since known as the &#34;sewer closet.&#34;</p><p>We won the battle and kept the carpet of the adjoining playroom clean and dry, but I lost the larger war, having to call in professional plumbers to clear out our sewer line the next day. The cause of the backup? Baby wipes. And only a few, mind you. Usually, our household doesn&#39;t flush wipes, but I had slacked a time or two and those few fateful flushes were all it took.</p><bi-shortcode id=\"related-article-module\" class=\"mceNonEditable\" data-type=\"5ac7c65f7ec3bb1b008b4a14\" data-title=\"The best hand soaps of 2021\" data-url=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/best-hand-soap\" data-thumbnail=\"https://i.insider.com/undefined\">Related Article Module: The best hand soaps of 2021</bi-shortcode><p>Disposal issues and plumbing catastrophes aside, over-relying on wet wipes is ethically questionable. Since most are nonbiodegradable, they linger in landfills and can potentially make their way into the ocean. So, what can you do if you love keeping clean with wet wipes (hey, all parents know that there&#39;s no law stipulating they&#39;re just for babies) but want to avoid the risk of causing damage to your toilet <em>and</em> the environment?</p><p>Well, there&#39;s the excellent option of converting your toilet paper into a wet wipe using <a href=\"https://shareasale.com/r.cfm?b=1319806&u=1088116&m=86257&urllink=fohm%2Eco%2F&afftrack=biipf%5F022219%5Ffohm%2Ddispenserfohm%2Ddispenser\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow\">Fohm</a>. No, not foam, Fohm. Although, Fohm <em>does</em> use foam. Let me explain. </p><p>The <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Ffohm.co%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored nofollow sponsored\">Fohm Co. starter kit</a> includes a touchless (and therefore hygienic) dispenser and a bottle of cleanser. The pH-balanced formula contains water, aloe, citric acid, and sulfates (this provides the foaming action), but is free of parabens, alcohol, and fragrance. The brand says the ingredients are quite close to what you&#39;d find in a baby wipe and that they&#39;re well-rated from the <a href=\"https://www.ewg.org/skindeep/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-saferedirecturl=\"https://www.google.com/url?q=https://www.ewg.org/skindeep/&source=gmail&ust=1583609437663000&usg=AFQjCNGMTQMTaeIn45vEmswumyzQcuKh1QwumyzQcuKh1Q\">Environmental Working Group&#39;s Skin Deep Directory</a>. </p><p>You simply hold toilet paper under the unit&#39;s sensor-operated nozzle and it automatically deposits a dollop of skin-safe foam, effectively turning it into a &#34;wet wipe.&#34; And once you&#39;re done with the DIY wet wipe, you can toss it into the toilet and flush away, knowing the paper will break down as it should, not clogging pipes or posing a risk to aquatic life down the line.</p><p>One more thing to note: as fancy as this system might seem, it actually saves you money in the long run. The starter pack costs $49, and after that, refills are $19 every three to five months (how often you&#39;ll need to re-up depends on the number of people in your household). This means a family of four could spend almost $7 on a single pack of baby wipes <em>or</em> put that money towards a month&#39;s worth of eco-friendly, plumbing-safe <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/reviews/out?u=https%3A%2F%2Ffohm.co%2F\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener nofollow nofollow sponsored\">Fohm</a> foam.</p><bi-shortcode id=\"commerce-link\" page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Officials in Georgia and Colorado have paused the distribution of the Johnson &#38; Johnson coronavirus vaccine at some vaccination sites after a few people experienced minor adverse reactions this week.</p><p>As The Denver Post <a href=\"https://www.denverpost.com/2021/04/07/vaccine-reaction-dicks-sporting-goods-park/\">reported Wednesday</a>, 11 people experienced reactions after receiving the J&#38;J shot at a mass-vaccination clinic in Commerce City, just north of Denver. With over 1,700 having being given the vaccine that day, that comes out to less than 1%.</p><p>On Thursday, Peter Banko, CEO of Centura Health, which was distributing the vaccines, said the company would pause while public health officials investigate whether there is an issue with the batch, <a href=\"https://twitter.com/MegWingerter/status/1380254196394496003\">The Post&#39;s Meg Wingerter reported</a>.</p><p>There were no issues earlier in the week, Wingerter noted.</p><p>Georgia&#39;s Department of Health announced it would pause its distribution of Johnson &#38; Johnson at a site in Cumming on Friday.</p><p>The Department of Health said eight people at the vaccination site experienced adverse reactions after receiving the Johnson &#38; Johnson vaccine on Wednesday. A total of 425 people had been given the Johnson &#38; Johnson vaccine that day.</p><p>&#34;There is no reason to believe there is anything wrong with the vaccine itself, and other individuals who have received the J&#38;J vaccine should not be concerned,&#34; DPH commissioner Kathleen Toomey said in a <a href=\"https://www.fox5atlanta.com/news/georgia-site-pauses-johnson-johnson-vaccine-use-after-adverse-reactions\">statement to Fox 5 Atlanta</a>. &#34;We are looking into what happened and what may have caused the reactions, including the conditions at the fairgrounds such as heat and the ability to keep the site cool.&#34;</p><p>Officials in North Carolina also temporarily paused its distribution of Johnson &#38; Johnson at several vaccination sites, but resumed its use of the vaccine on Friday.</p><p>Public health officials in Wake County had reported 14 people - out of more than 2,300 - <a href=\"https://twitter.com/MichaelWNCN/status/1380268147253579786\">experienced adverse reactions to the vaccine on Thursday. </a></p><p>After an investigation into the vaccine, health officials received an all-clear from the Centers from Disease Control and Prevention and resumed use of the vaccine,<a href=\"https://apnews.com/article/public-health-raleigh-north-carolina-coronavirus-pandemic-0f1f866dc2d2c10e7f7b848c396236e2\"> the Associated Press reported.</a></p><p>In a statement, Johnson &#38; Johnson told Insider it takes any adverse reactions seriously, saying it will &#34;carefully assess the events&#34; and share any findings with the Food and Drug Administration.</p><p>&#34;There is no burgers, is exploring a public listing that could give the company a valuation of $10 billion, <a href=\"https://www.reuters.com/article/us-impossible-foods-m-a-exclusive-idUSKBN2BV2SF\">Reuters reported</a> on Thursday.</p><p>At its last funding round in March 2020, the plant-based meat company was valued at <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/impossible-foods-raises-$500-million-at-nearly-$4-billion-valuation---source-8634005\">$4 billion</a>.</p><p>Impossible is now weighing options between going public via an initial public offering or a merger with a special-purpose acquisition company, Reuters said, citing sources. This could happen within a span of the next 12 months.</p><p>Financial advisers have been approached to help manage discussions with SPACs that have already extended offers at a lucrative valuation, sources told Reuters. The SPAC route could diminish the positions of existing shareholders more substantially compared to an IPO.</p><p>Impossible Foods was founded by CEO Pat Brown in 2011 when he was on a sabbatical from teaching biochemistry at Stanford University&#39;s medical school. Brown previously <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/impossible-foods-ceo-pat-brown-career-advice-2020-1\">told Insider</a> he wished he gained an understanding of the meat industry earlier in his career, so he could&#39;ve launched Impossible Foods sooner.</p><p>The company is backed by venture capitalists Khosla Ventures and Horizons Ventures, and more than a dozen superstar investors ranging from pop icon Katy Perry to tennis champion Serena Williams and rapper Jay-Z.</p><p>Shares in rival plant-based company <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/stocks/bynd-stock\">Beyond Meat</a> are trading more than 400% higher above its public debut price in 2019.</p><p>Several private companies are eager to be acquired by SPACs after a surge in popularity within the space last year. More than $98 billion has been raised across 306 SPAC IPOs so far in 2021, surpassing last year&#39;s record of $83 billion, according to <a href=\"https://spacinsider.com/stats/\">data from SPACInsider.com</a>.</p><p>Many of these companies may be unaware of the legal implications of not fully understanding the disclosures they can and can&#39;t make when going public. For this reason, the Securities and Exchange Commission has <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/spac-blank-check-merger-sec-official-blank-dealmakers-risks-complexities-2021-4-1030267783\">warned SPAC dealmakers</a> of the risks and governance issues related with raising capital through blank-check firms.</p><p>A spokesperson for Impossible declined to comment on the Reuters report.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the 00:41:45","updatedTime":"2021-04-10 00:41:45","title":"Gen Z's shopping habits are shaping the future of fashion: online thrifting","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/gen-z-driving-online-resale-secondhand-clothes-thrifting-poshmark-depop-2021-4","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606fc1114d3e410018b7025e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"gen z reselling clothes\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Gen Z is driving online resale.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Jamie Grill/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/gen-z-will-take-over-economy-2030-33-trillion-income-2020-11\">Gen Z</a> is making secondhand clothing cool thanks to its penchant for online resale.</li>\n<li>The $30 billion secondhand market is expected to grow 18% annually through 2024, per Jefferies.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/depop-sellers-turn-side-hustles-into-full-time-businesses-2020-2\">Buying used clothes</a> helps Gen Z avoid repeating outfits, practice sustainability, and make money.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>The future of fashion looks a lot like used clothes. Fueling the movement? Gen Z, of course.</p><p>The secondhand clothing market is a growing one. It&#39;s currently worth $30 billion, according to a recent Jefferies note, and is estimated to grow annually by 18% through 2024. About a quarter of the secondhand market is resale clothing, which Jefferies estimates to grow by 39% annually in the same time frame to eventually comprise over half of the market.</p><p>Based on these estimations, Jefferies forecasts the secondhand clothing market will comprise a mid-teen percentage of the overall apparel market over the next decade, driven by online resale, and when that happens, every other demographic will just be catching up to Gen Z, who&#39;s already there.</p><p>Look no further than social shopping apps like <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/poshmark-sellers-made-side-hustles-six-figure-businesses-2020-1\">Poshmark</a> and <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/depop-sellers-turn-side-hustles-into-full-time-businesses-2020-2\">Depop</a> for proof. Both have garnered large Gen Z user bases, who have taken to the apps to sell and buy secondhand clothing and accessories.</p><p>&#34;This company is for the next generation,&#34; Rachel Swidenbank, vice president of marketplace at Depop, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/teens-earn-money-fashion-depop-app-2019-4\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"20\" data-uri=\"87df5ed4bc51f3c3467e31cd5f88aa54\">previously told Insider&#39;s Mary Hanbury</a>. She said that 90% of Depop&#39;s users are under the age of 26.</p><p>Recycling and reselling clothes helps the digitally native generation wear new-to-them outfits on a budget they haven&#39;t yet posted to social, avoiding repeating looks. There, too, is the sustainable aspect of secondhand clothing - Gen Z is more willing than any other generation to pay more for sustainable products, according to a <a href=\"https://cdn2.hubspot.net/hubfs/160569/1.14.2020%20The%20State%20of%20Consumer%20Spending%20Gen%20Z%20Shoppers%20Demand%20Sustainable%20Retail.pdf?utm_campaign=Report%3A%20Generation%20Z%20Demands%20Sustainable%20Retail&utm_medium=email&_hsmi=81840717&_hsenc=p2ANqtz-8KnjMMpk6jXj5rZMQXtGXpayoLmYGW9K36iVFMnUEQJsSWcqzDgukq6CfjFcy3WhJo-BNMFhO8FPaCQmU-JWI6VB2nwQo7qxwJ2ALQmv9ocp7LH4k&utm_content=81840717&utm_source=hs_automationsource=hs_automation\" data-analytics-module=\"body_link\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"100\" data-uri=\"ac8941f14f4414f09f062776139608e8\">consumer spending analysis by First Insight</a>.</p><p>For active sellers, it&#39;s also a tool to start a lucrative side hustle. Depop sellers can pull in as much as $300,000 a year and have been able to buy houses and cars before they&#39;ve even reached college age, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/depop-sellers-turn-side-hustles-into-full-time-businesses-2020-2\">Swidenbank said</a>. And young sellers on Poshmark <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/poshmark-sellers-made-side-hustles-six-figure-businesses-2020-1\">told Insider&#39;s Jennifer Ortakales Dawkins</a> they were able to grow their resale hustle into a full-time business earning six figures or more in annual sales. </p><p>But even though Gen Z is driving the secondhand frenzy, they&#39;re not the only ones getting swept up in the trend. Emily Farra <a href=\"https://www.vogue.com/article/the-year-in-secondhand-vintage-upcycling-sustainable-fashion\">reported in November for Vogue</a> that secondhand, vintage, and upcycling caught steam in 2020. She cited Lyst&#39;s annual <a href=\"https://www.lyst.co.uk/year-in-fashion-2020\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\" data-event-click=\"{\"element\":\"ExternalLink\",\"outgoingURL\":\"https://www.lyst.co.uk/year-in-fashion-2020\"}co.uk/year-in-fashion-2020&#34;}\">Year in Fashion report</a>, which revealed a 35,000 increase in searches for &#34;vintage fashion&#34; and a 104% increase in entries for secondhand-related keywords in September.</p><p>Shoppers are rethinking their carbon footprint and looking for more unique pieces as clothing companies become more ubiquitous, she wrote, and brands are accommodating the rising interest. But there&#39;s also something to be said of the more subtle statement of a vintage piece of clothing over a flashy logo in a pandemic world.</p><p>As Farra wrote, &#34;In a difficult year that&#39;s seen staggering unemployment and countless shuttered businesses, the shift toward vintage and secondhand could come down to a desire for less-conspicuous fashion.&#34;</p><div 00:41:45","updatedTime":"2021-04-10 00:41:45","title":"Kim Kardashian West's shapewear line, Skims, is now worth over $1 billion after leaning into loungewear during the pandemic","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/kim-kardashian-west-skims-worth-over-1-billion-nyt-2021-4","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60704edc30004b0019b26d44?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Kim Kardashian Skims\" height=\"2052\" width=\"2730\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Kim Kardashian West at the launch of Skims at Nordstrom in New York City in February 2020.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Kevin Mazur/Getty Images for Nordstrom</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Kim Kardashian West&#39;s shapewear brand, Skims, is valued at $1.6 billion, The New York Times reports.</li>\n<li>Skims offers shapewear and loungewear that&#39;s inclusive of a range of sizes and skin tones.</li>\n<li>Kardashian West is worth $1 billion in her own right thanks to Skims and her KKW Beauty makeup line.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Kim Kardashian West&#39;s shapewear company has joined the unicorn club. </p><p>The 2-year-old brand, called Skims, has raised $154 million in new funding from Josh Kushner&#39;s Thrive Capital, as well as from existing investors, Imaginary Ventures and Alliance Consumer Growth. The new round pushes Skims&#39; valuation to $1.6 billion, Kardashian West told <a href=\"https://www.nytimes.com/2021/04/09/business/dealbook/kardashian-skims.html\">The New York Times&#39; Michael J. de la Merced</a>.</p><p>Kardashian West is Skims&#39; biggest shareholder and controls a majority stake along with her business partner, Jens Grede, The Times reports.</p><p>Skims&#39; billion-dollar valuation comes after a year when shoppers were less in need of shapewear and more in need of loungewear. But Skims had started introducing more laid-back apparel just as the pandemic hit in early 2020, inspired by Kardashian West&#39;s preference for being comfortable when she&#39;s in her house, <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=LALR0ovhVks\">she recently told Vogue</a>.</p><p>&#34;The pandemic hit at like, our first or second drop of loungewear, and we had loungewear designed for the whole next year to drop,&#34; she said. &#34;And it just happened to be the perfect time and the perfect storm of everyone staying home and wanting to just be a lot more comfortable.&#34; </p><p><em><strong>Read more: </strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/how-your-coronavirus-underwear-habits-are-claiming-an-unexpected-victim-2020-10\" data-e2e-name=\"inline-read-more-link\">COVID-19 has claimed an unlikely victim: Your underwear drawer. Here&#39;s why the industry expects a 12% sales dip in 2020.</a></em></p><p>But Kardashian West told The Times that shapewear is still at the core of Skims&#39; business, describing the company as &#34;your basics go-to.&#34; The company offers bras, underwear, bodysuits, shorts, slips, and even pregnancy support in a range of sizes (from XXS to 5X) and shades: Many of the shapewear items come in eight different flesh tones as well as black. </p><p>Despite challenges posed by the pandemic - like sourcing materials - Skims reported $145 million in sales in 2020, which it expects to double in 2021, according to The Times.</p><p>Skims&#39; new valuation follows Kardashian West&#39;s official debut as a billionaire. Earlier this week, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/kim-kardashian-net-worth-officially-billionaire-forbes-list-2021-4\">she appeared on Forbes&#39; billionaires list</a> for the first time, spurred by the success of Skims as well as her makeup line, KKW Beauty. Kardashian West <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/kim-kardashian-west-sells-20-stake-kkw-beauty-to-coty-2020-6\">sold a 20% stake in KKW Beauty</a> to makeup giant Coty in June 2020 in a deal that valued the brand at $1 billion. </p><p>Kardashian West also earns income from her family&#39;s reality show, &#34;Keeping Up With The Kardashians,&#34; which is on its final season, as well as endorsement deals, real estate holdings, business ventures like a now-defunct mobile app, and a portfolio of stocks that includes Disney, Amazon, and Netflix, <a href=\"https://www.forbes.com/sites/maddieberg/2021/04/06/kim-kardashian-west-is-officially-a-billionaire/?sh=43507f2621bb\">according to Forbes</a>.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original 2021 13:52:17 +0000","feedId":22,"bgimg":"https://i.insider.com/60704edc30004b0019b26d44?format=jpeg","linkMd5":"1e622789b2eb692158d0e7c0afde92af","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn36@2020_6/2021/04/09/16-41-45-860_60934550fb250e11.webp","destWidth":2730,"destHeight":2052,"sourceBytes":180874,"destBytes":180874,"author":"ahartmans@businessinsider.com (Avery Hartmans)","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://i.insider.com/60704edc30004b0019b26d44?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn36@2020_6/2021/04/09/16-41-45-860_60934550fb250e11.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn84@2020_2/2021/04/09/16-42-21-967_cc3ef43fc8ff5801.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=2LUs0iZKXQA:6DGKGHTxTIg:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn96@2020_5/2021/04/09/16-42-21-232_97c57b9b1522b25e.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=2LUs0iZKXQA:6DGKGHTxTIg:V_sGLiPBpWU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx24/cdn99@2020_6/2021/04/09/16-42-20-566_c01c399e8868dc55.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn91@2020_1/2021/04/09/16-42-19-669_740defb435ea442b.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=2LUs0iZKXQA:6DGKGHTxTIg:gIN9vFwOqvQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn96@2020_4/2021/04/09/16-42-19-334_678d05cbffad3c2b.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/businessinsider/~4/2LUs0iZKXQA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx3/cdn56@2020_5/2021/04/09/16-42-18-589_ffb0a420bad2cec9.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1617986505570},{"createdTime":"2021-04-10 00:41:45","updatedTime":"2021-04-10 00:41:45","title":"How a Bitcoin wallet gives you more security and control over your digital assets","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/bitcoin-wallet","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/607067f5f068cf0018022be5?format=jpeg\" alt=\"crypto wallet\" height=\"1249\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>A bitcoin wallet gives you, and only you, complete control of your cryptocurrency.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thana Prasongsin/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>A Bitcoin wallet is a digital app or program that allows you to securely send and receive bitcoins. </li>\n<li>Bitcoin wallets do not actually store funds, but instead store the private keys that give you access to your cryptocurrency.</li>\n<li>Bitcoin wallets come as either hardware or software, with hardware wallets offering the most security.</li>\n<li><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/investing-reference\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\" data-analytics-module=\"summary_bullets\" data-analytics-post-depth=\"0\" data-uri=\"1b4b1b102a76bd3c1b16e44162761b54\"><strong>Visit Business Insider&#39;s Investing Reference library for more stories.</strong></a></li>\n</ul><p>&#34;Not your keys, not your coin&#34; is a popular saying within some parts of the cryptocurrency community, and for good reason.</p><p>It&#39;s a reminder that if you choose to store your <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/what-is-bitcoin\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">bitcoin</a> on a cryptocurrency exchange account, the exchange actually owns the key to your digital assets. And if you don&#39;t own the private keys needed to transfer and access your bitcoin, you don&#39;t control it.</p><p>So how exactly do you control your keys and, by extension, your bitcoin? A dedicated Bitcoin wallet. </p><p>Bitcoin wallets are designed to store the private keys to your cryptocurrency, enabling you to move your funds without having to rely on a third-party. Here&#39;s what you need to know about what a Bitcoin wallet is and how it works. </p><h2><strong>What is a Bitcoin wallet?</strong></h2><p>A Bitcoin wallet is a software program that allows you to transfer and store bitcoin. Bitcoin isn&#39;t technically &#34;stored&#34; anywhere so the wallet actually stores a private security key that corresponds to the Bitcoin address of your wallet. The key is actually what gives you ownership and control of bitcoin stored in it, making it an invaluable tool as an investor.</p><p>A Bitcoin wallet is &#34;a way for you to store your digital keys, or access, to certain locations on the blockchain,&#34; says <a href=\"https://www.lexsokolin.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Lex Sokolin</a>, global fintech co-head at blockchain firm ConsenSys.</p><p>Similar to other cryptocurrencies, bitcoin is stored in addresses on its blockchain, which is essentially a ledger or database that can&#39;t be modified or erased. Each address has two keys (i.e., alphanumeric codes) associated with it, a public key and a private key. The public key is what other people can use to send bitcoin to it, and the private key is what you&#39;d use to send bitcoin from it.</p><p>This is precisely why some investors prefer storing their bitcoin on a wallet instead of a third-party platform.  A wallet holds the private key, which is necessary to validate that the true owner of a Bitcoin address is really requesting that bitcoin be sent from that address. </p><aside class=\"quick-tip headline-regular\"><p><strong>In the news: </strong>There is <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/currencies/news/bitcoin-price-btc-inaccessible-cryptocurrency-digital-currency-wallet-security-blockchain-2021-1-1029961482\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">$140 billion of inaccessible bitcoin</a> in the world  as a result to lost or locked-off crypto wallets. If you decide to buy a bitcoin wallet, it&#39;s extremely important to keep it and your password safe.</p></aside><h2><strong>Types of bitcoin wallets</strong></h2><p>All bitcoin and cryptocurrency wallets revolve around the storage of a private key. When it comes to wallets, you basically have two options: hardware or software.</p><h3>Hardware wallets</h3><p>Hardware wallets are generally small, handheld devices that store your bitcoin offline and can be plugged into your computer in order to verify transactions. &#34;A hardware wallet stores private keys through a device that is not your computer, while a software wallet runs on your computer or phone,&#34; says Sokolin.</p><p>Hardware wallets remain offline at all times (and are often referred to as &#34;cold&#34; wallets for this reason), theoretically making them safer when compared to their digital counterparts.</p><p>While the cost of hardware wallets vary from one manufacturer and model to another, wallets can generally range from $60 to $180. Wallets at the lower end of this spectrum will be just as secure as those at the more expensive end, although they may lack certain extra features, such as Bluetooth connectability and support for a wider range of cryptocurrencies.</p><h3>Software wallets</h3><p>Software wallets, also known as &#34;hot&#34; wallets, can be accessed either via a desktop browser or smartphone app. Whereas hardware wallets are used for long-term storage of large amounts, software wallets are better for storing smaller amounts and making daily spending and receiving payments convenient and fast.</p><p>&#34;A software wallet is an app on your phone or computer containing your private keys. Because it&#39;s usually connected to the internet, it&#39;s theoretically hackable, though the most reputable software wallets are considered extremely difficult to hack,&#34; says <a href=\"https://www.glengoodman.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Glen Goodman</a>, a cryptocurrency analyst and author of <em>The Crypto Trader.</em></p><p>Software wallets can come in three varieties:</p><ul><li><strong>Desktop wallets: </strong>These wallets are installed directly onto a computer, where the private keys are stored on its hard drive. Funds can be accessed only from that computer, allowing you to have full control over your wallet. </li><li aria-level=\"1\"><strong>Mobile wallets: </strong>These wallets function the same way as desktop wallets, but designed for the mobile experience. Mobile wallets are convenient and can be used on the go, but can carry a greater risk of malware.</li><li aria-level=\"1\"><strong>Web wallets: </strong>These are wallets that can be accessed through a web browser, oftentimes hosted by a provider who manages the security of your private keys. </li></ul><p>In theory, software wallets are more user-friendly than hardware alternatives, if only because they don&#39;t require you to keep track of the whereabouts of a physical device. Some software wallets also offer built-in trading features, so you can quickly sell your crypto through their app or desktop site.</p><p>Another advantage of the software wallet is that it can be cheaper than a hardware equivalent. Many of the most popular software wallets charge only transaction fees, which are set by the network of the cryptocurrency you&#39;re using. That said, with average bitcoin fees hitting as high as $30 during peak periods, multiple transactions can certainly take a bite out of your wallet.</p><aside class=\"quick-tip headline-regular\"><p><strong>Important:</strong> Paper wallets are an outdated and highly risky way to store your own bitcoin. As the name suggests, they&#39;re pieces of paper on which you write the private and public key to your Bitcoin address, which can be auto-generated using a dedicated website. </p></aside><h2><strong>Why are Bitcoin wallets so important?</strong></h2><p>The main advantage of a Bitcoin wallet is that it protects investors from potential cryptocurrency exchange hacks. While the major exchanges are improving their cybersecurity constantly, breaches <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.in/business/news/russian-cryptocurrency-exchange-livecoin-hacked-and-lost-control/articleshow/79962952.cms\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">still occur from time to time</a>, with Binance - the world&#39;s biggest exchange - being <a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/currencies/news/btc-binance-suffers-40-million-hack-2019-5-1028182318\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">hacked as recently as May 2019</a>.</p><p>&#34;If someone has a very large amount of cryptocurrency, an offline hardware wallet is a must. For people who only have small amounts of crypto, a decent software wallet can provide a reasonable level of security for most purposes&#34; says Goodman.</p><p>Having your own wallet means you&#39;re protected from potential hacks, and yet it also protects users from situations where an exchange freezes a customer&#39;s funds or account. For example, popular cryptocurrency exchange Coinbase <a href=\"https://help.coinbase.com/en/coinbase/other-topics/other/does-coinbase-freeze-accounts\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">acknowledges</a> that in &#34;extremely rare circumstances,&#34; it will prevent access to customer funds when required to comply with an order from a court or other authority.</p><aside class=\"breakout-box headline-regular\"><h2><strong>Best bitcoin wallets</strong></h2><p><strong><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606f846f30004b0019b26c77?format=jpeg\" alt=\"ledger wallet\" height=\"1666\" width=\"2222\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>The Ledger Nano S, a popular hardware wallet option.\n<p class=\"copyright\"><a href=\"https://www.gettyimages.com/detail/photo/ledger-hardware-wallet-for-cryptocurrency-with-royalty-free-image/951988442\" target=\"_blank\">AndreaAstes/Getty Images</a></p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure></strong></p><p>When it comes to hardware wallets, the two major brands are <a href=\"https://www.ledger.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Ledger</a> and <a href=\"https://trezor.io/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Trezor</a>. While these makers are reputable, there are a number of other brands worth checking out before you make a final decision.</p><ul><li><strong>Best overall:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.exodus.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Exodus</a></li><li><strong>Best for beginners: </strong><a href=\"https://shiftcrypto.ch/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Shift Crypto</a></li><li><strong>Best for advanced users:</strong> <a href=\"https://electrum.org/#home\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Electrum </a></li><li><strong>Best for mobile users:</strong> <a href=\"https://wallet.mycelium.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">MyCelium </a></li><li><strong>Best for Bitcoin-only users: </strong><a href=\"https://coinkite.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Coinkite</a></li></ul><p><br>For the full review and a complete rundown, check out our picks for the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/personal-finance/best-bitcoin-wallet\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">best Bitcoin wallets</a>. </p></aside><h2><strong>The financial takeaway</strong></h2><p>Bitcoin wallets are a great way to take full control of your cryptocurrency funds. The most secure wallets are hardware-based, since they involve the use of devices that never go online. That said, software wallets may afford a greater level of convenience and ease.</p><p>However, while cryptocurrency wallets help you gain control of your funds, they require you to step up your security game. You generally need to store hardware wallets - and their seed phrases - in secure places, otherwise you may have to kiss goodbye your bitcoin in the event of loss or theft.</p><bi-shortcode id=\"related-article-module-end-of-article\" class=\"mceNonEditable\"><a data-type=\"5fd2657a83bd0b4a7c28e05f\" data-title=\"What is Bitcoin?
